Dear colleagues!
We would like to bring to your kind attention that in the period from 3.00 p.m. to 4.00 p.m. on the 18th of February 2016 there will be a fire emergency TRAINING for employees of the Innopolis University at the educational and laboratory buildings. We ask you to be understanding of this event and when you will hear the alarm signal for fire emergency TRAINING, please go orderly downstairs to the READING HALL at the 1st FLOOR in the shortest possible time. We hope to fulfill the requirement of moving to the safe place in time and then, upon the receipt of training recall you will be able to continue your activities at the offices. Thank you in advance.

Best Regards,
Ildar Mukhutdinov
